- **P² terms:** 0.17/1.047 + 0.17/10.21 - 0.17/10.21 = 0.17/1.047 ≈ 0.1623

## GT Analysis

The GT numerical expression is:
```
0.17*(−1 + P/1.047)*(1 − P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 − P/10.21)*P + 0.17*(1 − exp(−0.097*P))*P
```

Let me expand this step by step.

**Term 1:** `0.17*(−1 + P/1.047)*(1 − P/10.21)*P`
= `0.17*(P/1.047 − 1)*(1 − P/10.21)*P`

Let me expand `(P/1.047 − 1)*(1 − P/10.21)`:
= `P/1.047 − P²/(1.047×10.21) − 1 + P/10.21`
= `−P²/10.69 + P/1.047 + P/10.21 − 1`
= `−P²/10.69 + P(1/1.047 + 1/10.21) − 1`

Multiply by `0.17*P`:
= `−0.17*P³/10.69 + 0.17*P²(1/1.047 + 1/10.21) − 0.17*P`

**Term 2:** `0.17*(1 − P/10.21)*P`
= `0.17*P − 0.17*P²/10.21`

**Term 3:** `0.17*(1 − exp(−0.097*P))*P`
= `0.17*P − 0.17*P*exp(−0.097*P)`

**Combining all terms:**

P³ coefficient: `−0.17/10.69 ≈ −0.0159`

P² coefficient: `0.17*(1/1.047 + 1/10.21) − 0.17/10.21`
= `0.17/1.047 + 0.17/10.21 − 0.17/10.21`
= `0.17/1.047 ≈ 0.1623`

P coefficient: `−0.17 + 0.17 + 0.17 = 0.17`

Exponential term: `−0.17*P*exp(−0.097*P)`

So GT = **a*P³ + b*P² + c*P + d*P*exp(e*P)** where e < 0.

This is: `c0*P³ + c1*P² + c2*P + c3*P*exp(c4*P)`

with specific constants.

Has an extra constant term c5. GT has no constant term (GT(0)=0). Setting c5=0 gives the right structure.
